2024-05-08 13:07:05 [distribute_process][init]  SELECT campaign_id , ag.agent_id , ag.first_name , ag.last_name , ag.img_path ,  ag.extension, t.team_name , group_name ,  count( calllist_id ) as total_call , sum( new_cnt ) as new_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as success_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as callback_cnt , sum( follow_cnt ) as follow_cnt , sum( dnc_cnt ) as dnc_cnt , sum( bad_cnt ) as bad_cnt FROM  (  select campaign_id ,agent_id ,calllist_id  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id IS NULL then 1 else 0 end as new_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 0 then 1 else 0 end as success_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 1 then 1 else 0 end as callback_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 2 then 1 else 0 end as follow_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 3 then 1 else 0 end as dnc_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 4 then 1 else 0 end as bad_cnt  FROM t_calllist_agent WHERE status = 1  ) AS a  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_agents ag ON a.agent_id = ag.agent_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_group g ON ag.group_id = g.group_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_team t ON ag.team_id = t.team_id  GROUP BY campaign_id ,agent_id

2024-05-08 13:07:14 [distribute_process][init]  SELECT campaign_id , ag.agent_id , ag.first_name , ag.last_name , ag.img_path ,  ag.extension, t.team_name , group_name ,  count( calllist_id ) as total_call , sum( new_cnt ) as new_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as success_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as callback_cnt , sum( follow_cnt ) as follow_cnt , sum( dnc_cnt ) as dnc_cnt , sum( bad_cnt ) as bad_cnt FROM  (  select campaign_id ,agent_id ,calllist_id  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id IS NULL then 1 else 0 end as new_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 0 then 1 else 0 end as success_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 1 then 1 else 0 end as callback_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 2 then 1 else 0 end as follow_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 3 then 1 else 0 end as dnc_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 4 then 1 else 0 end as bad_cnt  FROM t_calllist_agent WHERE status = 1  ) AS a  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_agents ag ON a.agent_id = ag.agent_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_group g ON ag.group_id = g.group_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_team t ON ag.team_id = t.team_id  GROUP BY campaign_id ,agent_id

2024-05-08 13:07:30 [distribute_process][init]  SELECT campaign_id , ag.agent_id , ag.first_name , ag.last_name , ag.img_path ,  ag.extension, t.team_name , group_name ,  count( calllist_id ) as total_call , sum( new_cnt ) as new_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as success_cnt , sum( callback_cnt ) as callback_cnt , sum( follow_cnt ) as follow_cnt , sum( dnc_cnt ) as dnc_cnt , sum( bad_cnt ) as bad_cnt FROM  (  select campaign_id ,agent_id ,calllist_id  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id IS NULL then 1 else 0 end as new_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 0 then 1 else 0 end as success_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 1 then 1 else 0 end as callback_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 2 then 1 else 0 end as follow_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 3 then 1 else 0 end as dnc_cnt  ,case when last_wrapup_option_id = 4 then 1 else 0 end as bad_cnt  FROM t_calllist_agent WHERE status = 1  ) AS a  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_agents ag ON a.agent_id = ag.agent_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_group g ON ag.group_id = g.group_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_team t ON ag.team_id = t.team_id  GROUP BY campaign_id ,agent_id
